            <script type="text/javascript">
             $(document).ready(function(){$("#derivat-tab1 .select-f11").change(function(){$(".tabs-style34 li").each(function(){if($(this).hasClass('selected')){var sel=$(this).children().attr("href").replace("#","");if(sel=="derivat-tab1"){var value=$("#derivat-tab1 .select-f11").val();loadMarketBlock('BSE',value);}else if(sel=="derivat-tab2"){var value=$("#derivat-tab2 .select-f11").val();loadMarketBlock('NSE',value);}}});});$("#derivat-tab2 .select-f11").change(function(){$(".tabs-style34 li").each(function(){if($(this).hasClass('selected')){var sel=$(this).children().attr("href").replace("#","");if(sel=="derivat-tab1"){var value=$("#derivat-tab1 .select-f11").val();loadMarketBlock('BSE',value);}else if(sel=="derivat-tab2"){var value=$("#derivat-tab2 .select-f11").val();loadMarketBlock('NSE',value);}}});});$("#stocks .tabs-style34 li a").click(function(){setTimeout(function(){$(".tabs-style34 li").each(function(){if($(this).hasClass('selected')){var sel=$(this).children().attr("href").replace("#","");if(sel=="derivat-tab1"){var value=$("#derivat-tab1 .select-f11").val();loadMarketBlock('BSE',value);}else if(sel=="derivat-tab2"){var value=$("#derivat-tab2 .select-f11").val();loadMarketBlock('NSE',value);}}});},200);});setTimeout(function(){checkMarketBlock();},200);});function checkMarketBlock(){$("#stocks .tabs-style34 li").each(function(){if($(this).hasClass('selected')){var sel=$(this).children().attr("href").replace("#","");if(sel=="derivat-tab1"){var value=$("#derivat-tab1 .select-f11").val();loadMarketBlock('BSE',value);}else if(sel=="derivat-tab2"){var value=$("#derivat-tab2 .select-f11").val();loadMarketBlock('NSE',value);}}});$("#tab-Stocks").addClass("selected");$("#tab-Derivatives").removeClass("selected");$("#tab-Commodities").removeClass("selected");}function loadMarketBlock(exchange,statisticType){var coCode='';$('#commodities').hide();$('#derivatives').hide();$('#stocks').show();$('ul#'+exchange.toLowerCase()+'-tabs li a').click(function(){$('ul#'+exchange.toLowerCase()+'-tabs li').removeClass('selected');$(this).parent('li').addClass('selected');});var ajaxUrl="/live-market/request-handler/home-page-market-data-ver1/cache-control/900/";if(statisticType=="most-viewed"){ajaxUrl="/live-market/request-handler/home-page-market-data-ver1";}$("#stocks img").each(function(){$(this).attr("src",$(this).attr("data-original"));$(this).removeAttr("data-original");});$.ajax({url:ajaxUrl,type:'GET',cache:false,data:"exchange="+exchange+"&statisticType="+statisticType,success:function(response){if(statisticType=='chart'){if(exchange=='BSE'){$('#bse-market-chart-container').html('');$('#bse-market-chart-container').html(response);$('#bse-market-tab-data').html('');}else if(exchange=='NSE'){$('#bse-market-chart-container').html('');$('#bse-market-chart-container').html(response);$('#nse-market-tab-data').html('');}}else{if(exchange=='BSE'){$('#bse-market-chart-container').html('');$('#bse-market-tab-data').html(response);}else if(exchange=='NSE'){$('#bse-market-chart-container').html('');$('#nse-market-tab-data').html(response);}}},error:function(){}});}
            </script>
